// ============non-terminal types=============
//  # => Integer
//  <assign> => Statement
//  <cast exp> => Exp
//  <class decl> => ClassDecl
//  <class decl>+ => List<ClassDecl>
//  <decl in class> => Decl
//  <decl in class>* => List<Decl>
//  <empty bracket pair> => Object
//  <empty paren pair> => Object
//  <exp5> => Exp
//  <exp6> => Exp
//  <exp7> => Exp
//  <exp8> => Exp
//  <exp> => Exp
//  <formal list> => VarDeclList
//  <inst var decl> => Decl
//  <list element> => VarDecl
//  <list element>* => List<VarDecl>
//  <local var decl> => Statement
//  <method decl> => Decl
//  <program> => Program
//  <return stmt> => Exp
//  <start> => void
//  <stmt> => Statement
//  <stmt>* => List<Statement>
//  <type> => Type
//  <unary exp> => Exp
//  CHARLIT => Integer
//  ID => String
//  INTLIT => Integer
//  STRINGLIT => String
//  `! => void
//  `!= => void
//  `% => void
//  `&& => void
//  `( => void
//  `) => void
//  `* => void
//  `+ => void
//  `++ => void
//  `, => void
//  `- => void
//  `-- => void
//  `. => void
//  `/ => void
//  `: => void
//  `; => void
//  `< => void
//  `<= => void
//  `= => void
//  `== => void
//  `> => void
//  `>= => void
//  `[ => void
//  `] => void
//  `abstract => void
//  `assert => void
//  `boolean => void
//  `break => void
//  `byte => void
//  `case => void
//  `catch => void
//  `char => void
//  `class => void
//  `const => void
//  `continue => void
//  `default => void
//  `do => void
//  `double => void

//  `extends => void

//  `final => void
//  `finally => void

//  `for => void
//  `goto => void

// ============productions (after empty-removal)=============
// 0: $$start ::= <start>
// 1: <start> ::= ws* <program>
// 2: <start> ::= <program>
// 3: <program> ::= <class decl>+
// 4: <class decl> ::= `class ID `{ <decl in class>* `}
// 5: <class decl> ::= `class ID `{ `}
// 6: <class decl> ::= `class `extends ID ID `{ <decl in class>* `}
// 7: <class decl> ::= `class `extends ID ID `{ `}
// 8: <decl in class> ::= <method decl>
// 9: <decl in class> ::= <inst var decl>
// 10: <method decl> ::= `public `void ID <formal list> `{ <stmt>* `}
// 11: <method decl> ::= `public `void ID <formal list> `{ `}
// 12: <method decl> ::= `public <type> ID <formal list> `{ <stmt>* <return stmt> `}
// 13: <method decl> ::= `public <type> ID <formal list> `{ <return stmt> `}
// 14: <type> ::= `int
// 15: <type> ::= `boolean
// 16: <type> ::= ID
// 17: <type> ::= <type> <empty bracket pair>
// 18: <empty bracket pair> ::= `[ `]
// 19: <empty paren pair> ::= `( `)
// 20: <formal list> ::= <empty paren pair>
// 21: <formal list> ::= `( <type> ID <list element>* `)
// 22: <formal list> ::= `( <type> ID `)
// 23: <list element> ::= `, <type> ID
// 24: <stmt> ::= <assign> `;
// 25: <stmt> ::= `{ <stmt>* `}
// 26: <stmt> ::= `{ `}
// 27: <stmt> ::= <local var decl> `;
// 28: <return stmt> ::= `return <exp> `;
// 29: <assign> ::= <exp> `= <exp>
// 30: <local var decl> ::= <type> ID `= <exp>
// 31: <inst var decl> ::= <type> ID `;
// 32: <exp> ::= <exp5>
// 33: <exp5> ::= <exp5> `+ <exp6>
// 34: <exp5> ::= <exp6>
// 35: <exp6> ::= <exp6> `* <exp7>
// 36: <exp6> ::= <exp7>
// 37: <exp7> ::= <cast exp>
// 38: <exp7> ::= <unary exp>
// 39: <cast exp> ::= `( <type> `) <cast exp>
// 40: <cast exp> ::= `( <type> `) <exp8>
// 41: <unary exp> ::= `- <unary exp>
// 42: <unary exp> ::= <exp8>
// 43: <exp8> ::= ID
// 44: <exp8> ::= <exp8> !<empty bracket pair> `[ <exp> `]
// 45: <exp8> ::= INTLIT
// 46: letter ::= {"A".."Z" "a".."z"}
// 47: letter128 ::= {193..218 225..250}
// 48: digit ::= {"0".."9"}
// 49: digit128 ::= {176..185}
// 50: ws ::= " "
// 51: ws ::= {10}
// 52: `boolean ::= "#" "b" "o" ws*
// 53: `boolean ::= "#" "b" "o"
// 54: `class ::= "#" "c" "l" ws*
// 55: `class ::= "#" "c" "l"
// 56: `extends ::= "#" "e" "x" ws*
// 57: `extends ::= "#" "e" "x"
// 58: `void ::= "#" "v" "o" ws*
// 59: `void ::= "#" "v" "o"
// 60: `int ::= "#" "i" "t" ws*
// 61: `int ::= "#" "i" "t"
// 62: `return ::= "#" "r" "e" ws*
// 63: `return ::= "#" "r" "e"
// 64: `public ::= "#" "p" "u" ws*
// 65: `public ::= "#" "p" "u"
// 66: `* ::= "*" ws*
// 67: `* ::= "*"
// 68: `( ::= "(" ws*
// 69: `( ::= "("
// 70: `) ::= ")" ws*
// 71: `) ::= ")"
// 72: `{ ::= "{" ws*
// 73: `{ ::= "{"
// 74: `} ::= "}" ws*
// 75: `} ::= "}"
// 76: `- ::= "-" ws*
// 77: `- ::= "-"
// 78: `+ ::= "+" ws*
// 79: `+ ::= "+"
// 80: `= ::= "=" ws*
// 81: `= ::= "="
// 82: `[ ::= "[" ws*
// 83: `[ ::= "["
// 84: `] ::= "]" ws*
// 85: `] ::= "]"
// 86: `, ::= "," ws*
// 87: `, ::= ","
// 88: `; ::= ";" ws*
// 89: `; ::= ";"
// 90: ID ::= letter128 ws*
// 91: ID ::= letter128
// 92: ID ::= letter idChar* $$0
// 93: ID ::= letter $$0
// 94: INTLIT ::= {"1".."9"} digit* $$1
// 95: INTLIT ::= {"1".."9"} $$1
// 96: INTLIT ::= digit128 ws*
// 97: INTLIT ::= digit128
// 98: INTLIT ::= "0" hexDigit* $$2
// 99: INTLIT ::= "0" $$2
// 100: idChar ::= letter
// 101: idChar ::= digit
// 102: idChar ::= "_"
// 103: idChar128 ::= letter128
// 104: idChar128 ::= digit128
// 105: idChar128 ::= {223}
// 106: hexDigit ::= {"0".."9" "A".."Z" "a".."z"}
// 107: hexDigit128 ::= {176..185 193..198 225..230}
// 108: <stmt>* ::= <stmt>* <stmt>
// 109: <stmt>* ::= <stmt>
// 110: <decl in class>* ::= <decl in class>* <decl in class>
// 111: <decl in class>* ::= <decl in class>
// 112: ws* ::= ws* ws
// 113: ws* ::= ws
// 114: digit* ::= digit* digit
// 115: digit* ::= digit
// 116: hexDigit* ::= hexDigit* hexDigit
// 117: hexDigit* ::= hexDigit
// 118: <list element>* ::= <list element>* <list element>
// 119: <list element>* ::= <list element>
// 120: idChar* ::= idChar* idChar
// 121: idChar* ::= idChar
// 122: <class decl>+ ::= <class decl>
// 123: <class decl>+ ::= <class decl>+ <class decl>
// 124: $$0 ::= idChar128 ws*
// 125: $$0 ::= idChar128
// 126: $$1 ::= digit128 ws*
// 127: $$1 ::= digit128
// 128: $$2 ::= hexDigit128 ws*
// 129: $$2 ::= hexDigit128

**** STATE 0 ****
    $$start ::= <%> <start> // $
    -----------------------
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ <decl in class>* `} // $
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ <decl in class>* `} // <class decl>
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ [<decl in class>*] `} // $
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ [<decl in class>*] `} // <class decl>
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class `extends ID [#] ID `{ <decl in class>* `} // $
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class `extends ID [#] ID `{ <decl in class>* `} // <class decl>
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class `extends ID [#] ID `{ [<decl in class>*] `} // $
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class `extends ID [#] ID `{ [<decl in class>*] `} // <class decl>
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl> // $
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl> // <class decl>
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl>+ <class decl> // $
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl>+ <class decl> // <class decl>
    <program> ::= [#] <%> <class decl>+ // $
    <start> ::= <%> ws* <program> // $
    <start> ::= [ws*] <%> <program> // $
    `class ::= <%> "#" "c" "l" [ws*] // ID
    `class ::= <%> "#" "c" "l" [ws*] // `extends
    `class ::= <%> "#" "c" "l" ws* // ID
    `class ::= <%> "#" "c" "l" ws* // `extends
    ws ::= <%> " " // <program>
    ws ::= <%> " " // ws
    ws ::= <%> {10} [registerNewline] // <program>
    ws ::= <%> {10} [registerNewline] // ws
    ws* ::= <%> ws* ws // <program>
    ws* ::= <%> ws* ws // ws
    ws* ::= [ws*] <%> ws // <program>
    ws* ::= [ws*] <%> ws // ws
